SQL> WHERE emp.deptno = dept.deptno;
SP2-0734: "WHERE emp...."(으)로 시작되는 알 수 없는 명령 - 나머지 줄은 무시되었습니다.
SQL> SELECT empno, ename, deptno, deptno, dname, loc
  2  FROM emp, dept
  3  WHERE emp.deptno = dept.deptno;
SELECT empno, ename, deptno, deptno, dname, loc
                             *

15 개의 행이 선택되었습니다.

SQL> -----NUM 2-----

SQL> SELECT E.ENAME, E.SAL, E.DEPTNO, D.DEPT_AVG_SAL
  2  FROM emp E
  3  JOIN (
  4      SELECT DEPTNO, AVG(SAL) AS DEPT_AVG_SAL
  5      FROM emp
  6      GROUP BY DEPTNO
  7  ) D
  8  ON E.DEPTNO = D.DEPTNO
  9  WHERE E.SAL > D.DEPT_AVG_SAL
 10  ORDER BY E.ENAME;

ENAME             SAL     DEPTNO DEPT_AVG_SAL                                   
---------- ---------- ---------- ------------                                   
ALLEN            1600         30   1566.66667                                   
BLAKE            2850         30   1566.66667                                   
FORD             3000         20         2175                                   
JONES            2975         20         2175                                   
KING             5000         10         2800                                   
SCOTT            3000         20         2175                                   

6 개의 행이 선택되었습니다.

SQL> SELECT E1.ENAME AS "이름", E1.DEPTNO AS "부서번호",
  2         E2.ENAME AS "상사이름", E2.DEPTNO AS "상사부서"
  3  FROM emp E1
  4  JOIN emp E2 ON E1.MGR = E2.EMPNO
  5  ORDER BY E1.ENAME;

15 개의 행이 선택되었습니다.

SQL> -----NUM 4-----
SQL> SELECT E.ENAME, E.DEPTNO, E.SAL
  2  FROM emp E
  3  JOIN (
  4      SELECT DEPTNO, MAX(SAL) AS MAX_SAL
  5      FROM emp
  6      GROUP BY DEPTNO
  7  ) D
  8  ON E.DEPTNO = D.DEPTNO AND E.SAL = D.MAX_SAL
  9  ORDER BY E.DEPTNO;

ENAME          DEPTNO        SAL                                                
---------- ---------- ----------                                                
KING               10       5000                                                
SCOTT              20       3000                                                
FORD               20       3000                                                
BLAKE              30       2850
